### Create a file

```bash
>take-the-command-challenge
:>take-the-command-challenge
.>take-the-command-challenge
0>take-the-command-challenge
*>take-the-command-challenge
>take-the-command-challenge;
->take-the-command-challenge
>>take-the-command-challenge
> take-the-command-challenge
>take-the-command-challenge .
cd>take-the-command-challenge
: >take-the-command-challenge
>> take-the-command-challenge
*> take-the-command-challenge
.> take-the-command-challenge
:> take-the-command-challenge
> take-the-command-challenge;
cd >take-the-command-challenge
nul>take-the-command-challenge
a > take-the-command-challenge
- > take-the-command-challenge
: > take-the-command-challenge
> take-the-command-challenge .
cd.>take-the-command-challenge
> ./take-the-command-challenge
. > take-the-command-challenge
cd> take-the-command-challenge
cd .>take-the-command-challenge
ca >>take-the-command-challenge
' ' >take-the-command-challenge
cd.@>take-the-command-challenge
nul >take-the-command-challenge
cd :>take-the-command-challenge
cd. >take-the-command-challenge
vi > take-the-command-challenge
CD > take-the-command-challenge
nul> take-the-command-challenge
$cat>take-the-command-challenge
"" > take-the-command-challenge
cd > take-the-command-challenge
```

### find string

```bash
grep G *
grep G a*
grep G<*g

cat * |grep GET
```

```bash
cat access.log | sort | cat
cat access.log | sort -k1,1
cat access.log | uniq | sort

cat access.log | sort access.log
ls access.log | sort -n access.log
cat `find . -name access.log` | sort
find . -name *access.log* | xargs cat -
cat /var/challenges/simple_sort/access.log
find . -name "access.log" | sort access.log
find . -name access.log -exec sort '{}' ';'
cat `find . -name "access.log*" -print` | sort
find "access.log" -type f -exec cat {} + | sort
find . -type f -name "access.log*" -exec cat {} +
```

### replace spaces

```bash
ls|tr " " .

ls *\ *|tr \ .
ls |tr ' ' '.'

ls|sed 's/ /\./g'
ls -1 |tr ' ' '.'
ls -r |tr ' ' '.'
ls| sed 's/ /./g'
ls| sed 's| |.|g'
ls -1 | tr ' ' '.'

ls -h | tr " " "."
tr ' ' '.' < <(ls)
ls ** | tr ' ' '.'
ls | sed 's_ _._g'
ls -1 * | tr ' ' .
ls|sed 's/\ /\./g'
ls -A | tr ' ' '.'
ls | sed "s\ \.\g"
ls -r |tr ' ' '\.'
ls | sed "s/ /./g"

ls -r | tr ' ' '.'
find * | tr ' ' '.'
```

### print common lines

```bash
awk 'f[$1]++{print$1}' *
awk 'f[$1]++{print $1}' *
awk 'a[$1]++{print $1}' *
awk 'a[$1]++ {print $1}' *
awk 'f[$1]++{print $1}' a*

cut -d\ -f1 *|sort|uniq -d
awk 's[$1]++{print $1}' a*
awk 'seen[$1]++{print$1}' *
cut -f1 -d' ' *|sort|uniq -d
awk 'seen[$1]++{print $1}' *
awk 's[$1] ++ {print $1}' a*
cut -f1 -d' ' * |sort|uniq -d
awk 'test[$1]++{print $1}' a*
awk 'f[$ 1] ++ {print $ 1}' *
cut -f1 * -d' '|sort| uniq -d
cut -d ' ' -f 1 *|sort|uniq -d
cut -f1 * -d' ' |sort| uniq -d
awk 's[$1]++' a*|cut -d' ' -f1
awk 'count[$1]++{print $1}' a*
cut -f1 -d' ' * | sort |uniq -d
sort *|grep -o ^[0-9.]*|uniq -d
awk 's [$ 1] ++ {print $ 1}' a*
cut -f1 -d' ' * | sort | uniq -d
```

```bash
cat file-with-tabs.txt| grep -P "\t" | wc -l
cat file-with-tabs.txt |grep -P "\t" | wc -l
cat file-with-tabs.txt | grep -P "\t" | wc -l

cat file-with-tabs.txt | grep -P '\t' | wc -l
grep -c "$(printf '\011')" file-with-tabs.txt
```
